# Changelog ŌĆö 2026-06

### 2026-06-22 ŌĆö fix(charly): `charly bundle del <pod>` was broken ŌĆö record-free teardown via `charly remove`

`charly bundle del <pod>` ALWAYS errored `"no container deploy named X in ledger"`. RCA: `PodUnifiedTarget.Del`
(unified_targets_pod.go) was built on a ledger-DeployRecord teardown model that pods never use ŌĆö the ONLY
DeployRecord writer is `VmDeployTarget` (deploy_target_vm.go:181, `Target="vm:"+name`); a pod bakes its candies
into an overlay image and persists charly.yml state, writing NO deploy record. So `findContainerDeploy` always
returned nil and Del errored before tearing anything down (the bug never surfaced because the check beds tear
down with `charly remove`, not `charly bundle del`). The path was also INCOMPLETE ŌĆö it stopped+rm'd the
container but never removed the quadlet or the charly.yml entry, and its overlay check
(`strings.HasSuffix(ref, "-overlay")`) couldn't match the real `<name>-overlay:<tag>` ref.

Fixed: Del is now RECORD-FREE. It delegates the container + quadlet + sidecar + charly.yml cleanup to the
canonical `charly remove` path (consistent with the sibling lifecycle delegations Start/Stop/Update ŌĆö R3), then
drops the deploy's synthesized `<name>-overlay:*` images (the one extra `bundle del` does over `charly remove`;
a shared base ref is never named that, so it is preserved) and cancels any ephemeral TTL lifecycle. DELETED the
dead `findContainerDeploy` (Del was its only caller) and corrected the stale install_ledger.go Target-field
comment (the same false `container:<name>` claim ŌĆö R5). New regression test
`TestPodUnifiedTarget_Del_DelegatesToRemove` asserts the `remove <name>` delegation.

R10 (live, disposable check-pod): `bundle add check-pod` + config + start ŌåÆ running; `bundle del check-pod` ŌåÆ
EXIT 0, container removed + quadlet removed + charly.yml entry cleaned + base image preserved (was: always
errored). `go test ./...` (incl. the new test) + `task build:charly` green. Surfaced during the
charly-core-externalization triage (the findContainerDeploy follow-up, upgraded from a dead-code note to a real
bug).

### 2026-06-22 ŌĆö refactor(charly): collapse the duplicated volume host-path strategy into one helper (PP5)

`ResolveVolumeBacking` (deploy.go) carried the bind/encrypted host-path strategy switch TWICE ŌĆö once for
label-matched volumes (keyed by the short name) and once for deploy-only volumes (keyed by the config name) ŌĆö
byte-identical apart from that name argument. Extracted to ONE `resolveVolumeHostPath(dv, name, storageDir,
encStoragePath, volumesPath)` helper (R3); both passes call it. Behavior-identical (the only varying input is
now an explicit parameter); no exported-signature change, callers unchanged. The gocryptfs encrypted LIFECYCLE
stays core (a volume-backing provider class was correctly deferred ŌĆö single backend, deeply wired into
start/quadlet/credential). Also FIXED a standing R1 divergence: two `enc_test.go` comments promised tests at
`deploy_test.go (TestResolveVolumeBacking*)` that never existed ŌĆö WRITTEN now (table-driven
`TestResolveVolumeBacking_HostPath` covering bind/encrypted ├Ś default/host, plus `TestResolveVolumeBacking`
covering named-fallthrough + label-matched + deploy-only), making the comments true. R10: go test (the new
tests) + check-pod (ResolveVolumeBacking drives every pod deploy, fresh `charly update`). Wave-1 **PP5** of the
charly-core-externalization program.

### 2026-06-22 ŌĆö refactor(charly): delete the dead deploy-target legacy-spelling alias residue (P3)

EDGE-INHERIT / schema-v4 left runtime alias-following for the legacy deploy-target spellings
(`container`ŌåÆ`pod`, `kubernetes`ŌåÆ`k8s`, `host`ŌåÆ`local`), but the runtime NEVER sees them: `BundleNode.Target`
is set only by `bundleTargetForDisc` from the node-form kind at the edge (always canonical
pod|vm|k8s|local|android), `charly migrate` (schema-v4 + target-local) rewrites the legacy spellings
on-disk, and the loader hard-rejects un-migrated configs. The alias-following was pure dead
belt-and-suspenders. Deleted: the legacy-spelling switch arms in `classifyTarget` (deploy_tree.go) and
`classifyNodeTarget` (bundle_add_cmd.go); the now-no-op `canonicalDeployWord` (unified_targets.go); the three
`RegisterBuiltinAlias(ClassDeployTarget, ŌĆ”)` calls (deploy_builtins.go); and ŌĆö deploy-target being its ONLY
user ŌĆö the whole registry alias mechanism (the `aliases` map, `RegisterBuiltinAlias`, and `resolve`'s alias
branch in provider_registry.go). Canonical dispatch is unchanged (`resolve` is a plain byKey lookup;
`checkDeployProviderBijection` iterates canonical words). Also corrected a stale migration-status comment that
claimed kinds/steps/builders are "still switch-driven" (C2/C4/C5 landed). KEPT (separate concerns, not this
claim): the name-based fallbacks (a deploy literally NAMED `host`/`local` ŌåÆ local) and the persisted-ledger
`container:`-key reader `findContainerDeploy` (deploy-record state-format, its own future assessment).

R10: go test ./... + check-pod + check-local (each resolves its canonical target through the now alias-free
registry, on a fresh `charly update`). Wave-1 **P3** of the charly-core-externalization program ŌĆö corrected
from the audit's "route through the registry" (which assumed the aliases were live) to an R5 dead-residue
deletion after RDD proved them unreachable.

### 2026-06-22 ŌĆö fix(charly): enforce the plugin protocol-version gate on connect (was claimed, never performed)

`buildUnit` (the client-side construction lifting a connected plugin's `Describe` reply into a
`*PluginUnit`) read only `caps.GetProvided()` + `caps.GetSchemaCue()` and SILENTLY DISCARDED the
`Capabilities.protocol_version` + `calver` fields the server sends ŌĆö while a comment in `connectAndDescribe`
asserted "a gross mismatch is a readable refusal rather than a wire panic." No refusal code existed: a plugin
built against a different charly proto/SDK connected silently and failed later as a wire panic. Fixed:
`buildUnit` now enforces `caps.GetProtocolVersion() == sdk.ProtocolVersion` and refuses a mismatch with a
readable error naming the plugin's protocol, its (advisory) CalVer, and the host's required protocol. CalVer
is NOT an equality gate ŌĆö plugins are independent repos at independent CalVers, and a same-host builtin served
out-of-process may advertise an empty CalVer (identical binary) ŌĆö so it is surfaced in the diagnostic only.
The false comment is replaced with a truthful one; `TestBuildUnitRefusesProtocolMismatch` covers the refusal,
`TestPluginGRPCRoundTrip` the accept path. R10: `check-pod` (the external out-of-tree plugin advertises the
matching protocol ŌåÆ bed green with the gate active). Wave-1 **PE4** of the charly-core-externalization
program (`~/.claude/plans/charly-core-externalization.md`).

### 2026-06-21 ŌĆö fix(charly): `charly vm ssh` connects via the managed ssh_config alias, not `localhost:2222` (cutover-B finding)

`charly vm ssh <name>` reconstructed the ssh invocation by hand ŌĆö `ssh -p <port> <user>@localhost`, the port
DEFAULTING to 2222 and resolved only from the vm spec's `SSH.Port`. For a `port_auto` VM the auto-allocated host
port lives in `VmDeployState`, NOT the spec, so the resolution missed it and fell back to `localhost:2222` ŌĆö
connecting to the wrong port. Fixed: `vm ssh` now execs `ssh <vmName>`, the MANAGED ssh_config Host alias
(`charly-<box>[-<instance>]`) published at `charly vm create` (`publishVmSshAlias`), which resolves the user,
the host port (including the auto-allocated one), and the generated key from `~/.config/charly/ssh_config`. This
DELETES the duplicate manual port/key resolution (R3 ŌĆö the alias is the single managed SSH interface); `-l`/`-p`
still override. Live-verified: on a fresh `port_auto` k3s-vm (resolved port 35423, not 2222), `charly vm ssh
k3s-vm echo ŌĆ”` connected through the alias and ran the command. Found during cutover B's cachyos-vm investigation.

### 2026-06-21 ŌĆö fix(charly): drop the stale `host` (C) + `box` (D) kind words from the wrong-kind-child gate

EDGE-INHERIT residual cleanup (a cutover-C + cutover-D follow-up). The wrong-kind-child gate's HARDCODED
kind lists had drifted: `node_parse.go` listed `host` among the deployable kinds (cutover C removed the
`host:` venue kind) and `box` among the non-deployable kinds (cutover D merged `box:` into `candy:`), and
`node_bundle.go`'s resource-member error listed `host`. Corrected to the current kinds ŌĆö deployable:
`pod/vm/k8s/local/android/group`; non-deployable: `candy/distro/ŌĆ”`; resource members:
`pod/vm/k8s/local/android`. `resourceKindSet` itself is CUE-derived (`spec.ResourceKinds`) and was already
correct ŌĆö only the hardcoded error/comment STRINGS were stale, so there is no behavior change (an invalid
config was already rejected; only the message text was wrong). Live-verified: `charly box validate` on a
wrong-kind-child config now emits the corrected list. The check skill's reserved-kind list drops `host` too.

### 2026-06-21 ŌĆö feat(charly)!: EDGE-INHERIT cutover D ŌĆö the `box:` KIND merged into `candy:` (`base:`/`from:` presence = image)

The fourth and LARGEST EDGE-INHERIT cutover, completing the program ("kinds live only at config EDGES").
The `box:` KIND keyword is ELIMINATED ŌĆö merged INTO `candy:`. There is now ONE entity kind: a `candy:` node
carrying `base:` (an external base) or `from:` (a builder ref) is a full IMAGE (the former `box:`); a `candy:`
with neither is a LAYER fragment. The `charly box build/validate/...` COMMAND family is UNCHANGED (a command,
not a kind ŌĆö like `charly bundle` survived cutover B).

**The loader.** `candyKind.DecodeNode` routes a `candy:` node by `candyIsImage` (the `base` OR `from` marker
ŌĆö the corpus has 75 boxes with `base:`, 4 bootstrap builders with `from: builder:ŌĆ”` and no base, and zero
layers using `from:`) into `uf.Box` (BoxConfig) vs `uf.Candy` (InlineCandy) ŌĆö the existing SEPARATE maps, so
the boxŌŖĢcandy name reuses (redis, nvidia, jupyter, ŌĆ”) need ZERO renames. `boxKind` is deleted; `box` leaves
`_reservedNode`/`#Node`.

**The schema ŌĆö the implicit-discriminator hazard the design panel flagged, resolved.** A raw `(#Candy | #Box)`
disjunction is NOT concretely validatable: in CUE a required-but-absent field is INCOMPLETE, not BOTTOM, so a
no-base/no-from layer never eliminates the image arm. Fix: `#Image: #Box & ({base!} | {from!})` (the image arm
REQUIRES baseŌŖ╗from) and `#CandyValue: (*#Candy | #Image)` ŌĆö the `*#Candy` DEFAULT resolves it (an image carries
base/from ŌåÆ bottoms closed `#Candy` ŌåÆ `#Image`; a layer ŌåÆ the default `#Candy` wins). `candy.cue`'s `from:` is
removed (it is now an image marker on `#Box`).

**The migration.** New `box-to-candy` step (`renameBoxDisc`: `box:`ŌåÆ`candy:` at every KIND discriminator,
scoped to MAPPING-valued discriminators so a `box:` cross-ref FIELD is never touched) ŌåÆ HEAD `2026.172.0006`;
the corpus is migrated + re-stamped across the superproject + all 5 `box/<distro>` submodules + the per-host
overlay.

**Four production bugs the box/candy merge surfaced, each RCA'd and fixed in this cutover:** (1) `validate.go`
validated images against the now-deleted `cueKindDef("box")` ŌåÆ `box`ŌåÆ`#Box` re-registered as an INTERNAL
validation key (cueKindDefs is not bijective with the kind keywords); (2) the disjunction concrete-validation
(the `*#Candy` default above); (3) `renameBoxDisc` over-reached onto the `box:` IMAGE cross-ref FIELD of
`#K8s`/`#Android` ŌåÆ scoped to mapping-valued discriminators; (4) `applyDiscoveredManifest` had its OWN `candy:`
discovery branch missing the `candyIsImage` check, so discovered IMAGES landed in `uf.Candy` ŌĆö breaking
`charly box list`/`box build` for every submodule (`&& !candyIsImage(gn)` added). The `AddBox` scaffold is
rewritten from the stale kind-keyed `box:` to node-form `<name>: {candy: {base:}}`. The `candy:`-as-CHILD =
composition behavior (classifyDisc's `asChild`) is correct and preserved ŌĆö an image/layer can never be a
deploy member.

Docs (CLAUDE.md + 93 SKILL.md + README) swept of the `box:` kind, with strict MUST-form authoring guidance
(an IMAGE MUST be a `candy:` carrying `base:`/`from:`; the `charly box` COMMAND is unchanged). R10 (all
fresh-rebuild gates green): check-local + check-pod + check-k3s-vm + check-arch-vscode-pod +
check-debian-coder-pod + check-ubuntu-coder-pod + check-cachyos-vm.

**Follow-ups found (each its own next cutover):** `#K8s`/`#Android`'s image cross-ref FIELD is still spelled
`box:` (should be `image:`, a cutover-B gap); the `host` kind word still appears in `node_parse.go`'s
wrong-kind-child error message + the check skill's reserved-kind list (a cutover-C residual).

### 2026-06-21 ŌĆö feat(charly)!: EDGE-INHERIT cutover C ŌĆö eliminate the `host:` venue kind; rename Calamares `group` ŌåÆ `package-group`

The third EDGE-INHERIT cutover ŌĆö a ZERO-CORPUS schema refactor (the `host:` venue kind and the Calamares
`group:` both have zero on-disk usage, so there is no migration / re-stamp; the schema change is in-place,
no HEAD bump).

**C.1 ŌĆö the `host:` venue KIND is GONE.** A remote/host deploy is the `host:` FIELD on a `local:` deploy
(`local: {from: <template>, host: <user@machine>}`), never a standalone `host:` venue node. `#HostValue` +
`#HostArm` are deleted from node.cue; `host` leaves `_reservedNode` + `#ResourceKind`; the `bundleKind`
provider (its last user ŌĆö `bundle` went in cutover B, `host` now) is deleted; and the DEAD config-derived
`host` disc/target branches (`node_bundle.go` `bundleTargetForDisc`, `deploy_tree.go` `deriveChildExecutor`,
`deploy_chain.go` `appendHopForFlatPath`) are removed. The internal runtime "host" EXECUTION-venue label
(the host MACHINE ŌĆö a separate concept, not a config kind) is unchanged.

**C.2 ŌĆö the Calamares package group moves to its own `package-group:` kind.** `group:` is now UNAMBIGUOUSLY
the targetless DEPLOY group (resource members, no own workload ŌĆö the former targetless `bundle:`); the
cutover-B dual-mode shape-routing in `groupKind.DecodeNode` is gone, and a new `packageGroupKind` decodes
`#Group` into `uf.Group`. `cueKindDefs` realigned: `group`ŌåÆ`#Deploy`, `package-group`ŌåÆ`#Group` (was the
stale `group`ŌåÆ`#Group`, which would have validated a deploy group against the Calamares def ŌĆö a latent
zero-corpus bug fixed here). The `target.cue` `group?: [...string]` FIELD (package-group names) is unchanged.

Skills + CLAUDE.md swept of the `host:` venue kind + the `group:` dual-mode, and given strict MUST-form
authoring guidance (a host deploy MUST be `local: {host: ŌĆ”}`; a Calamares group MUST be `package-group:`).
The migrate skill table is backfilled with the cutover-A/B step rows + the correct HEAD. R10 (all
fresh-rebuild gates green): check-local + check-pod + check-k3s-vm.

### 2026-06-21 ŌĆö feat(charly)!: EDGE-INHERIT cutover B ŌĆö `bundle:` kind eliminated; substrate kinds at the EDGE with `from:`/`image:` cross-refs

The second cutover of the EDGE-INHERIT program ("kinds live only at config EDGES, never in the middle").
The `bundle:` deploy KIND keyword is GONE: a deploy now carries its SUBSTRATE KIND directly at the edge ŌĆö
`pod:` / `vm:` / `k8s:` / `local:` / `android:` for a workload, or `group:` for a targetless group of
members. The six cross-ref FIELDS `box?`/`pod?`/`vm?`/`k8s?`/`local?`/`android?` collapse to two: `image:`
(the box/OCI image a `pod`/`k8s`/`android` RUNS ŌĆö the former `box:`) and `from:` (inherit a SAME-kind
template by name ŌĆö the former `vm:`/`k8s:`/`local:`/`android:` cross-refs). So `bundle:{box:web}`ŌåÆ
`pod:{image:web}`, `bundle:{vm:pg}`ŌåÆ`vm:{from:pg}`, and a targetless `bundle:{disposable:true,ŌĆ”}`ŌåÆ
`group:{ŌĆ”}`.

The substrate kinds serve DOUBLE duty (a `vm:` is EITHER a VmSpec template with `source:` OR a deploy with
`from:`/`image:`), resolved by SHAPE in the loader (`standaloneKind.DecodeNode` routes on `isDeployShape`:
a scalar disc value or a `from:`/`image:` field ŌåÆ a deploy; bare ŌåÆ a template); `group:` is dual-mode too
(the Calamares package group vs a targetless deploy group, routed by resource members). The RDD spike that
opened the cutover proved the CUE DISJUNCTION arm resolves template-XOR-deploy cleanly, so `VmSpec` and
`BundleNode` stay SEPARATE Go types ŌĆö the ripple is just the cross-ref fields, NOT a 480-ref restructure.
CUE `#Deploy` loses the six cross-refs (gains `from?`/`image?`); `#BundleArm`/`#BundleValue`/the `bundle`
reserved word are deleted from `node.cue`; `group` joins `#ResourceKind` (a deploy group nests members,
its Calamares-subgroup `subgroup:` being a FIELD, not a `group:` child, so no collision). The Go ripple is
the receiver-scoped cross-ref renames (`.Box`ŌåÆ`.Image`, `.Vm`/`.K8s`/`.Local`/`.Android`ŌåÆ`.From`) across
the loader, deploy targets, status collectors, and commands; `inferBundleTarget`/`setBundleCrossRef` are
rewritten (the disc IS the target ŌĆö no inference) and the `bundle` kind provider deleted. The save-path
serialization (`bundleDiscForEntity`) emits the substrate kind from `Target`.

A new idempotent `charly migrate` step `edge-inherit` (RECURSING into nested members) raises the schema
HEAD to `2026.172.0004`; the whole corpus (the main `charly.yml`, candies, every `box/<distro>` submodule,
and the per-host overlay) is migrated `bundle:`ŌåÆsubstrate. The earlier F3 host-overlay-pollution class
DISSOLVES ŌĆö a check-local bed is now a plain `local:` deploy node, not a `bundle:` carrying a `local:`
cross-ref. Skills + CLAUDE.md swept of the `bundle:` KIND (the `charly bundle` command + the `BundleNode`
Go type are unchanged).

The full bed-roster R10 surfaced a PRE-EXISTING VM-deploy race (NOT caused by the node-form change ŌĆö the
FIRST deploy passed on the same tree): `check-cachyos-vm`'s fresh-rebuild hit `pacman -Sy: unable to lock
database` because cloud-init's first-boot seed-package install still held `/var/lib/pacman/db.lck` ŌĆö
`WaitForCloudInit` cleared on a blank/transient `cloud-init status` read before `cloud-final.service`
finished. RCA'd and fixed GENERICALLY for every VM substrate (arch/cachyos/debian/ubuntu/fedora share the
injected `{openssh,curl,tar}` seed packages, so a cachyos-only cloud-init patch would be an R3 sibling
hack): `WaitForCloudInit` now gates on an explicit TERMINAL cloud-init state (done/error/disabled), and a
new R4 `WaitForPackageLock` sync primitive blocks the deploy until no boot-time pacman/apt/dnf process
holds the lock. R10: check-local + check-pod + check-k3s-vm + check-arch-vscode-pod + check-debian-coder-pod
+ check-ubuntu-coder-pod + check-cachyos-vm disposable beds pass on the fresh substrate form (the two VM
beds re-run on the package-lock fix).

### 2026-06-21 ŌĆö feat(charly)!: EDGE-INHERIT cutover A ŌĆö step probe verbs `k8s`/`group` renamed to `kube`/`unix_group` (no kind word mid-config)

The first cutover of the EDGE-INHERIT program ("kinds live only at config EDGES, never in the middle").
Two declarative check-step PROBE VERBS reused reserved KIND words: `k8s:` (cluster probe) collided with
the `k8s` deploy substrate, and `group:` (getent unix group / groupadd) with the Calamares `group` kind.
They are renamed to `kube:` / `unix_group:` everywhere ŌĆö the `#OpVerb` vocabulary + `#Op` fields (`.Kube`,
`.UnixGroup`, the kube verb's `kube_*` modifiers, the `#KubeMethod` enum, all regenerated from the
single-source `schema/_common.cue` via `task cue:gen`), the `VerbCatalog` + `liveVerbDispatch` registry
keys, the verb-provider registrations (`kubeVerb`/`unixGroupVerb`, `runKube`/`runUnixGroup`/`kubeMethods`),
and the CLI subcommand `charly check k8s <method>` ŌåÆ `charly check kube <method>` (`KubeCmd`). The `k8s`
deploy KIND, the `k8s:` bundle cross-ref, and the Calamares `group` kind are UNTOUCHED (only the verb
namespace moved). New machine-checks `spec/TestNoKindWordAsStepVerb` + `TestNoKindWordAsOpModifier` fail the
build if any future step verb/modifier is spelled like a kind word. A new idempotent `charly migrate` step
`probe-verb-rename` (gated on `isStepNode` so only plan-step `k8s:`/`group:`/`k8s_*:` keys move, never the
deploy kind) raises the schema HEAD to `2026.172.0002`; the whole corpus (the main `charly.yml`, candies,
and every `box/<distro>` submodule) is re-stamped and the `check-k3s-vm` plan + `box/arch`'s `group: wheel`
check are migrated. Skills updated with strict MUST-form guidance (a step verb may never collide with a
kind word). Also fixes a pre-existing bed-infra bug surfaced by the R10: `persistBedDeployOverrides` no
longer persists a LOCAL bed to the global per-host overlay ŌĆö a local bed never runs `charly config` (its
only reason to seed) and its `local:` template lives in the bed's own project, so writing it poisoned every
OTHER project's overlay load (`validateCheckBeds: references local template ŌĆ” not defined`), breaking
concurrent `check-pod`/`check-k3s-vm` runs. Local deploys persist via the install ledger, so the skip is
lossless.

### 2026-06-21 ŌĆö feat(charly)!: unified plugin schema over the Describe channel ŌĆö `.cue` single source, zero builtin/external distinction

A plugin's `.cue` schema is now the SINGLE SOURCE used two ways, IDENTICALLY for a built-in (in-proc)
and an out-of-tree (out-of-proc) plugin: at DEV time `cue exp gengotypes` produces the plugin's Go param
struct (the provider decodes `plugin_input` into it, never a hand-parsed map); at RUNTIME the plugin
SERVES its `.cue` source over the Provider `Describe` RPC (the new proto `Capabilities.schema_cue` +
structured `ProvidedCapability{class,word,input_def}`), and the host splices it onto its base schema
(`base ++ plugin`) and validates every authored `plugin_input` against the plugin's def. The host NEVER
reads a candy's `schema/` dir from disk ŌĆö the schema travels WITH the plugin. Both kinds arrive as a
`PluginUnit{Providers,Schema}` from `PluginTransport.Connect` (`InProcTransport` for a builtin,
`LocalTransport` for an external), so the load/gate/validate code never branches: `registerPluginUnitSchema`
is the ONE load gate (empty / non-spliceable / missing-def ŌåÆ loud failure; builtins gated at process start
via `loadBuiltinPluginUnits`, externals at connect), and `validateAuthoredPluginInput` is the ONE validator,
wired into `runPluginVerb`. The reference built-in moves into charly's module as a self-contained unit
(`charly/plugin/builtins/exampleprobe/`: schema + gen'd params + `Schema()`/`InputDefs`), and the external
example serves via the new `sdk.BuildCapabilities` (embeds + compiles its schema standalone, ships the
source). `task cue:gen` regenerates every plugin's params from its `.cue` (new `schemagen -pkg` flag + a
loop over `charly/plugin/builtins/*/schema` + the in-repo external). The check-runner now loads plugins
from the RESOLVED candy set (`ScanAllCandyWithConfig`, which includes `@github`-fetched candies and carries
each candy's `.Plugin` + `.SourceDir`) instead of `LoadUnified`'s project-local map ŌĆö so a box that vendors
all its candies via `@github` (every `box/<distro>`) loads its plugins; `buildPluginBinary` flattens an
`@github`-ref candy key to a safe binary filename. DELETED (R5): `compileBasePlusPlugin` (the disk-read
splice), `charly/schema/plugin_example.cue` + `spec.ExampleprobeInput` (the builtin-schema-in-core-spec
path), `buildProviders`, the old `validatePluginInput`, the proto `repeated string provided`. R10:
`check-pod` composes the built-in (`exampleprobe-baked`) AND the external plugin (`externalprobe-out-of-proc`)
ŌĆö fresh `charly check run check-pod` PASS (steps=10), both plugins dispatching through the unified
schema-over-RPC mechanism, the external out-of-process with its marker round-tripping.

---

### 2026-06-21 ŌĆö fix(charly): bundle-node plan steps now run under `charly check live` (the pod path)

A pod bundle's OWN authored plan steps (a bed's `status-shows-pod` check, or any `check:` on the bundle
node) were SILENTLY NOT RUN under `charly check live` ŌĆö `CheckLiveCmd.Run` (the pod path) merged only the
baked candy/box plan + the per-host deploy overlay, never the PROJECT bundle's plan. The VM path
(`loadVmCheckPlans`) and the local path (`runLocalCheck`) already merged it; only the pod path diverged.
The fix mirrors them: the pod check-live composition now also merges `uf.ProjectBundleConfig()`'s bundle
plan (`projectPlan + localPlan`, the per-host overlay replacing by id) into the set. Found during C0 ŌĆö
the `exampleprobe` check had to be baked into the box plan to run on a pod bed; with this fix a
bundle-node check runs too. R10: check-pod runs `status-shows-pod` under check-live (previously absent ŌĆö
check-live went 8ŌåÆ10 steps, PASS); check-local's `status-shows-local` (the already-correct local path)
confirms no regression.

---

### 2026-06-21 ŌĆö refactor(charly): InstallPlan steps ŌåÆ provider registry (delete 3 type-switches + dead WalkPlan)

C4 of the plugin program ŌĆö the LAST switch migration: the 3 per-step type-switches (OCI `emitStep` in
build_target_oci.go, local `execStep` in deploy_target_local.go, the VM `emitPlan` loop in
deploy_target_vm.go) are replaced by the provider registry. Each of the 12 InstallStep kinds is a
`StepProvider` (`step_builtins.go`) with `EmitOCI`/`EmitLocal`/`EmitVM` methods preserving their venue's
EXACT prior behaviour cell-by-cell ŌĆö the gate checks (RepoChange hard-errors without
`--allow-repo-changes`; services silent-skip without `--with-services`), the per-VM-cell ReverseOp
collection, and the apk/reboot per-venue skips; the per-target `emitX`/`execX` handlers are unchanged.
The dispatch sites resolve via `providerRegistry.ResolveStep(step.Kind())` and call the matching method;
a bijection (`checkStepProviderBijection`) asserts every kind has a provider. The DEAD, never-wired
`walk_plan.go` (`WalkPlan` + `StepExecutor` ŌĆö a "Phase 1 defined, Phase 2 never done" abstraction
covering only 8 of 12 kinds) is DELETED (R3). Behavior-preserving ŌĆö proven by the full install/emit/
deploy test suite. R5: `git grep 'case *ApkInstallStep:'` / `WalkPlan` / `StepExecutor` ŌåÆ only
`CHANGELOG/`. R10: check-pod (OCI emit) + check-k3s-vm (VM emitPlan) + check-local (local execStep),
fresh-rebuild.

### 2026-06-21 ŌĆö refactor(charly): builders ŌåÆ provider registry (delete BuilderImageResolver + 3 builder switches)

C5 of the plugin program: the 3 per-builder switches + the dead injected resolver are replaced by the
provider registry. Each built-in builder (aur/pixi/cargo/npm) is a `BuilderProvider`
(`builder_builtins.go`) carrying its UNCHANGED `Reverse` (teardown ops) + `CollectContext` (per-builder
stage context); `BuilderStep.Reverse` + `collectBuilderContext` resolve via
`providerRegistry.ResolveBuilder`. The aur staging special-case (the `if s.Builder == "aur"` guard in
execBuilder) becomes a `BuilderStager` method (aur ŌåÆ `/tmp/aur-pkgs`). The injected
`BuilderImageResolver` func (local + vm targets, the tier-3 fallback) was NEVER wired in production ŌĆö
deleted, leaving the 2-tier overrideŌåÆcompiled-step resolution. A custom candy builder has no provider ŌåÆ
falls through (no reverse op, base context only); builders have no CUE vocabulary, so no bijection gate.
Behavior-preserving. R5: `git grep BuilderImageResolver` + the builder `case "aur":` ŌåÆ only `CHANGELOG/`.
R10: `install_plan_test` exercises `Reverse` for all 4 builders through the registry (+ aur_replaces_test,
generate_test's OCI aur stage, vm_builder_xhost_test) and check-jupyter-pod builds the
`jupyter-pixi-build` stage (collectBuilderContext + the OCI pixi builder stage) live on a disposable bed.

### 2026-06-21 ŌĆö refactor(charly): check verbs ŌåÆ provider registry (delete the runOne dispatch switch)

(`checkVerbProviderBijection`, run after registration to avoid the alphabetical init-order race)
asserts every check-dispatch `spec.OpVerb` has a provider ŌĆö the pure-install verbs
(mkdir/copy/write/link/download/setcap/build) are excluded (they render to install steps, not

### 2026-06-21 ŌĆö feat(charly): plugin-system foundation ŌĆö ONE unified Provider over the reserved-word registry

First cutover of the plugin program (`~/Atrapub/charly-plugin.md`): a single `Provider`
abstraction keyed by reserved word, generalizing the CUE-single-source reserved-word registry
so every kind/verb (and future deploy/step/builder) is one Provider ŌĆö in-process (built-in) OR
out-of-process (go-plugin gRPC), resolved identically by call sites (transport-invisible).

- **`provider.go` / `provider_registry.go`** ŌĆö the `Provider` interface (`Reserved`/`Class`/
  `Invoke` + the `Operation`/`Result` envelope) and `reservedProviders`, keyed by (class, word)
  because a word like `k8s` is both a kind and a verb. `RegisterBuiltinProvider` (init()) +
  `RegisterPluginProviders` (out-of-proc).
- **The generic `plugin:` check verb** ŌĆö `#OpVerb`/`#Op` gain `plugin`/`plugin_input`; `runOne`
  ŌåÆ `runPluginVerb` ŌåÆ `providerRegistry.ResolveVerb`. An out-of-tree plugin's verb is authorable
  without recompiling `Op`; an unresolved plugin verb FAILS (never fake-greens).
- **Plugins are candies** ŌĆö `#Candy.plugin:` (`{providers, source}`) + `validatePluginCandy`
  (a builtin provider must be compiled in); a plugin candy needs no install files. The reference
  built-in plugin `candy/plugin-example` provides + tests the `exampleprobe` verb.
- **go-plugin v1.8.0 + grpc v1.61.0 + protobuf** (grpc pinned to go-plugin's k8s-safe minimum ŌĆö
  forcing v1.81.1 downgraded `k8s.io/client-go` to alpha); `charly/plugin/proto` (the uniform
  Invoke envelope, JSON payloads so `spec` stays the single source) + `taskfiles/Proto.yml`
  (checksum-pinned protoc, reproducible); `LocalTransport` + `charly __plugin serve|list`.

Internal dispatch switches (check-verb / kind / deploy / step / builder) migrate in later
cutovers; the out-of-proc git-repo-plugin lifecycle (ExecutorTransport, runtime schema splice,
label discovery) + the bundle-overlay-step-not-running finding are the immediate follow-ups.
R10: check-pod bakes + runs the `exampleprobe` plugin verb on a disposable bed (fresh-rebuild).
Bumps the `box/fedora` gitlink to the matching bed coverage.

### 2026-06-21 ŌĆö feat(charly): the init system is a true single-source OCI label (`ai.opencharly.init_def`)

Closes the R3 duplication where the init entrypoint + management commands lived in BOTH the embedded `init:` vocabulary (build-time, but its `entrypoint:`/`fallback_entrypoint:` keys had become DEAD ŌĆö no runtime consumer after the go-quality cutover deleted `initEntrypointArgs`) AND the hardcoded `wellKnownInitDefs` registry (runtime), because the build-time vocab is unavailable at deploy (only the OCI-label init NAME was).

- **New label `ai.opencharly.init_def`** (`labels.go`) carries a dedicated `CapabilityInitDef` JSON subset ŌĆö `entrypoint`, `fallback_entrypoint`, `management_tool`, `management_commands` ŌĆö so build-only `InitDef` fields never leak into the deploy contract. Added per the capabilities recipe: `BoxMetadata.InitDef *CapabilityInitDef` + `CapabilityLabelMap` entry (enforced by `TestCapabilityLabelCompleteness`).
- **Baked at build** in `writeLabels` (`generate.go`) from the vocab-resolved `labelInitDef` (the same `ResolveInitSystem` that already produced `LabelInit`); **read label-first at deploy** ŌĆö `resolveEntrypointFromMeta` (`start.go`) + `resolveInitDefFromMeta` (`service.go`) consult `meta.InitDef` first.
- **`wellKnownInitDefs` retained ONLY as the legacy fallback** for pre-label images (cannot re-bake an already-built image's labels ŌĆö R5 doesn't apply to a still-needed backcompat path); its doc rewritten to say so, and the table frozen (new init systems are declared in the vocab, not added here).
- **Capability win:** the dead vocab `entrypoint:`/`fallback_entrypoint:`/`management_*` keys are now LIVE (consumed ŌåÆ label), and **custom init systems declared only in the vocab now work at RUNTIME** (their full contract travels in the label ŌĆö previously "build-only"). The stale "honored at build only" comments + skill notes are corrected.

Runtime class: `golangci-lint` 0, `go build/vet/test` (5 new tests: round-trip, legacy-fallback for supervisord+systemd, custom-init-at-runtime, capability completeness), `task cue:gen` reproducible, `charly box validate`. R8: a freshly-built supervisord image carries the label (`charly box labels ŌĆ” --format ai.opencharly.init_def` ŌåÆ the resolved entrypoint + management commands) and the deployed quadlet's `Exec=supervisord -n -c /etc/supervisord.conf` derives from it. R10: the `check-pod` disposable bed end-to-end (`PASS`, 10 steps incl. fresh-rebuild; host clean). Bumps the `plugins` gitlink to the matching skill updates.

### 2026-06-20 ŌĆö chore(charly): go-quality cleanup ŌĆö golangci-lint to zero + gofmt

Resolved the full charly Go-quality backlog (the go-quality skill's 1017-issue baseline is STALE ŌĆö the real audit was 13 `golangci-lint` findings + 9 `gofmt` files; the tree has been heavily cleaned since, partly by the CUE-single-source cutover deleting offending code). All fixed MANUALLY (never `golangci-lint --fix` ŌĆö it corrupts this tree) with adversarial default-refute triage:

- **5 staticcheck `QF1012`** (`internal/schemagen`) ŌåÆ `fmt.Fprintf` (proven output-stable by `TestGenReproducible`).
- **4 `unconvert`** (`config.go` ├Ś3, `intermediates.go`) ŌĆö redundant `[]string(...)` on fields already `[]string` (the generated `spec.Box.Build`).
- **1 `unparam` `specSource`** ŌĆö dropped the never-used `[]string` return (both callers discarded it).
- **1 `unparam` `builderPhaseTemplate`** (phase always `PhaseInstall`) ŌåÆ `//nolint:unparam` (reasoned): it's the uniform-signature `BuilderDef` analog of `formatPhaseTemplate` (which DOES vary phase via `s.Phase`); the three-phase machinery is documented forward design (`install_build.go:505`), no builder authors `prepare:`/`cleanup:` yet ŌĆö removing the param would delete reachable schema-backed generality.
- **1 `gocyclo` `(*Op).VerbsSet`** (47) ŌåÆ `//nolint:gocyclo` (reasoned): the skill's exact flat exactly-one-verb enumeration archetype; extraction would relocate cases without clarifying.
- **1 `unused` `initEntrypointArgs`** ŌåÆ DELETED. RCA (skill: an unused unexported func may be a latent missing-caller bug): `git log --all -S "EntrypointArgs("` proves `InitDef.EntrypointArgs` was NEVER wired in any commit (the CUE cutover free-func'd an already-dead method); the runtime entrypoint resolves exclusively from the separate hardcoded `wellKnownInitDefs` registry (`service.go:131`), so the func is unreachable by construction ŌĆö genuinely dead, not a regression.
- **`gofmt -w`** on 9 files (7 test files + `schemagen/main.go` + `spec/hand_state_types.go`) ŌĆö AST-identical.

Gate: `golangci-lint run ./...` = **0 issues**, `gofmt -l .` empty, `go build/vet/test` green, `TestGenReproducible` (pinned cue v0.16.1) byte-identical, `charly box validate`, and the `check-pod` disposable bed end-to-end (`PASS`, 10 steps incl. fresh-rebuild; host clean). No `plugins` change. Candidate follow-up surfaced (non-blocking): the embedded vocab's init `entrypoint:`/`fallback_entrypoint:` keys now have no Go consumer (they were already dead) ŌĆö delete or annotate in a later cutover.

### 2026-06-20 ŌĆö fix(charly): deploy-config state correctness ŌĆö idempotent migrate of a kind-named node + VM-bed entry teardown

Two deploy-config state-handling bugs the prior cutover's R10 surfaced (no authored format change ŌåÆ no schema bump):

- **`migrate --dry-run` perpetually (wrongly) reported `would apply unified-node`** on the repo's own root `charly.yml`. RCA: the repo has a node-form entity literally NAMED `vm` (`vm: {vm: {source: ŌĆ”}}` ŌĆö a valid node-form VM entity whose name collides with the `vm` kind keyword), and `migrateUnifiedNodeDoc` keyed on `legacyKindMapKeys["vm"]` and re-ran the legacy-kind-map rewrite path on it, rebuilding to byte-identical output but returning `changed=true`. Fix (`migrate_unified_node.go`): skip a top-level kind-word entry whose value is ALREADY node-form ŌĆö `!legacyKindMapKeys[k] || (nodeShapedValue(v) && !mapHasKey(v,"name"))`. A genuine legacy collection (`vm: {arch: ŌĆ”, cachyos: ŌĆ”}`, entity-name children) is not `nodeShapedValue` and still converts; a legacy single-entity (`vm: {name: ŌĆ”}`) keeps its `name:` key and still converts. `charly migrate --dry-run` from the repo root now reports `nothing to migrate`.
- **`removeVmDeployEntry` leaked a stale bundle entry** for a `kind: check` VM bed. RCA: a check-VM bed (`check-k3s-vm`) WRITES its `vm_state` under the BUNDLE key (`check-k3s-vm`), but every teardown caller REMOVES the prefixed VM-entity key (`vm:k3s-vm`) ŌĆö an exact-key lookup that missed, so the domain was destroyed but the config entry leaked (and the entry carried no `vm:` cross-ref to resolve it back). Fix (`bundle_add_cmd_vm.go`): `saveVmDeployState` gains a `vmEntity` param and persists `entry.Vm` (the cross-ref linkage); `removeVmDeployEntry` resolves the actual written key(s) via `vmDeployEntryKeys` ŌĆö the literal name AND every bundle whose `vm:` cross-ref names the entity ŌĆö with no over-match.

Runtime class: `go test ./...` (3 new tests incl. node-named-`vm` idempotency, legacy-collection-still-converts, bundle-keyed-entry-removal), `task cue:gen` reproducible, `charly box validate`, repo-root `migrate --dry-run` clean, and the `check-k3s-vm` disposable VM bed end-to-end (`PASS`, 6 phases incl. fresh-rebuild + full k3s suite; **post-teardown the host config has zero `check-k3s-vm` entries** and the fix also cleaned the pre-existing leaked entry; no orphan domain; 8 unrelated entries survived). No `plugins` change.

### 2026-06-20 ŌĆö fix(charly): harden the per-host migrate path ŌĆö empty-dir relocate orphan, testdata skip, vm-state write lock, `ov_install_strategy` key

Follow-up to the CUE-single-source cutover: five per-host migrate-path residuals the R10 bed gate surfaced (none changed an authored wire key).

- **Empty-`~/.config/charly`-dir relocate orphan** (`migrate_charly_rebrand.go`): `relocateHostStateForCharly` retargeted `ctx.HostDeployPath` onto `~/.config/charly` even when the `~/.config/ov ŌåÆ ~/.config/charly` move was SKIPPED because `~/.config/charly` already existed (empty), orphaning the real overlay at `~/.config/ov/deploy.yml` and no-op'ing the chain on a phantom path (`charly migrate` silently recovered nothing). New `mergeHostStateDir(from,to)` moves every non-conflicting top-level entry into the empty/lacking target (NEVER clobbering a pre-existing entry) then removes the emptied source ŌĆö so a host in that state recovers with no manual `rmdir`.
- **Migrate walked `charly/testdata`** (non-idempotent dev-repo noise): R3-unified the two duplicated candidate scanners into one `migrateCandidateYAMLFiles` (`migrate_walk.go`) that skips any `testdata` path component (alongside the existing nested-submodule skip); `opUnifyCandidateFiles` + `dropBoxPortCandidateFiles` now delegate to it. ALL doc-migration steps honor the skip (197 candidates, 0 testdata).
- **`saveVmDeployState` lost-update race** (`bundle_add_cmd_vm.go`): the VM-state read-modify-write now takes the same blocking `acquireDeployConfigLock` `saveDeployState`/`cleanDeployEntry` use (applied to `removeVmDeployEntry` too); reentrancy-audited ŌĆö no caller holds the lock, so no self-deadlock (flock per-open-fd).
- **`ov_install_strategy` ŌåÆ `charly_install_strategy`** vm_state key (`migrate_install_strategy_key.go`): new `install-strategy-key` migration step at intra-HEAD CalVer `2026.169.0002` (between `unified-node` and `step-venue`) renames the key at every depth on project files AND the per-host overlay; a reflection test pins the rename target to the live `spec.VmDeployState` yaml tag. NO `LatestSchemaVersion` bump ŌĆö this COMPLETES the already-landed 2026.159 ovŌåÆcharly rebrand's coverage of an internal deploy-state key, not a new format (HEAD stays `2026.169.0004`; a HEAD bump was empirically proven wrong ŌĆö it breaks `box validate` on the superproject + 5 box submodules already at HEAD).

Runtime class: `go test ./...` (8 new tests incl. concurrent-writers-all-survive, orphan-recovery, testdata-skip, key-rename + struct-tag pin), `task cue:gen` reproducible, `charly box validate`, and the `check-k3s-vm` disposable VM bed end-to-end (`PASS (steps=6)`, the now-locked `persist-auto-port` allocating + persisting + reusing SSH port 44949 with no self-deadlock; host clean after, no orphan domain). Bumps the `plugins` gitlink to the matching migrate-skill note. Two orthogonal pre-existing issues were observed and left for a separate cutover (a `migrateUnifiedNodeDoc` root-`charly.yml` dry-run non-idempotency present on `main`; `removeVmDeployEntry` targeting the `vm:` key not a bundle key).

### 2026-06-20 ŌĆö refactor(charly): CUE `schema/*.cue` is the single source of truth ŌĆö Go param structs + reserved-word vocabulary are GENERATED (gengotypes reversal)

**`charly/schema/*.cue` is now the SINGLE SOURCE OF TRUTH for the `charly.yml` ingress grammar.** The Go param structs, the reserved-word vocabulary, and the kind/verb wiring are GENERATED or DERIVED from the CUE defs ŌĆö there are no hand-maintained parallel copies. `task cue:gen` regenerates the new `charly/spec` package from `charly/schema/*.cue`; `charly/spec/cue_types_gen.go` is emitted by **`cue exp gengotypes`** (then yaml-retagged), and `charly/spec_aliases.go` repoints every package-main param type to its generated twin via `type X = spec.X` (`BoxConfig`, `Op`, `CandyYAML`, `VmSpec`, `ServiceEntry`, ŌĆ”) so the **Go compiler itself is the field-parity check** ŌĆö a renamed or dropped spec field fails the build at that surface.

**The long-standing do-NOT-use-`gengotypes` guidance is REVERSED.** The former `/charly-internals:go` point-5 rule ("Do NOT generate the Go structs with `cue exp gengotypes` ŌĆö it generalizes disjunctions to `any` and remaps names; keep the hand lockstep instead") no longer holds. The precision loss is handled at the source: every lossy CUE disjunction is annotated `@go(-)` to suppress its generated type, and the faithful Go union/shorthand/state type is hand-written in the SAME `spec` package (`spec/union_types.go`, `spec/scalar_aliases.go`, `spec/hand_state_types.go`) and referenced by name. The committed generated Go can never drift from the schema ŌĆö `charly/spec/gen_repro_test.go` re-runs the exact `task cue:gen` toolchain into a temp dir and diffs against the committed `cue_types_gen.go` + `vocab_gen.go` (skipping gracefully when the pinned `cue` CLI is absent).

**The reserved-word vocabulary + per-verb method allowlists are DERIVED from CUE, and the eight hand vocab lists are DELETED.** `charly/spec/vocab_gen.go` (emitted by the companion generator `charly/internal/schemagen` `-mode=vocab`, via the embedded `cuelang.org/go` API) carries the single-source slices ŌĆö `KindWords`, `ResourceKinds`, `DocDirectives`, `StepKeywords`, `ContextWords`, `DataKeys`, `OpFields`, `OpVerbs`, `AuthoringVerbs`, and the `LiveVerbMethods` allowlist map. The eight hand-maintained lists that previously hard-coded the same words are gone ŌĆö `kindKeys`/`kindKeysSet`, `rootShapeKeys`, `docDirectiveKeys` (`unified.go`) and `nodeEntityKinds`, `nodeResourceKinds`, `nodeStepVerbs`, `nodeDataKeys`, `nodeDocDirectives` (`node_parse.go`) ŌĆö replaced by `kindWordSet` / `resourceKindSet` / `stepKeywordSet` / `dataKeySet` / `docDirectiveSet` set-views in `reserved_registry.go`. The schema concatenation is unified in the new leaf package `charly/internal/schemaconcat`: ONE `ConcatSchema` that both the runtime (`cue_schema.go`'s `sharedCueSchema`) and the dev-time generator call, so the validated schema and the generated types can never diverge.

**A reserved-wordŌåÆhandler registry + a startup bijection gate enforce that every kind/verb is wired.** `charly/reserved_registry.go` binds each kind word to its CUE def (`"vm" ŌåÆ "#Vm"`), each verb to its `VerbCatalog` entry, and each live-verb method to its `liveVerbDispatch` handler; its `init()` runs three bijection checks fail-fast at process start (mirrored as `TestReservedWordRegistry_{KindBijection,VerbBijection,MethodAllowlists,KindsDispatchable}` in `reserved_registry_test.go`) ŌĆö `checkKindBijection`, `checkVerbBijection`, `checkMethodAllowlists` ŌĆö so a kind/verb/method can no longer be added to the schema without a handler, nor a handler survive its word's deletion.

**`#NodeDoc` is the sole load-time grammar gate; the legacy kind-keyed/root-shape routing and `keylint.go` are DELETED.** `mergeUnifiedDocs` runs every document ŌĆö root `charly.yml` and discovered manifests alike ŌĆö through `classifyDoc` ŌåÆ the closed `#NodeDoc` CUE gate ŌåÆ `normalizeNodeInto`; a legacy kind-keyed / root-shape document is no longer routed but HARD-REJECTED with a `charly migrate` hint (the `mergeKindDoc` / `firstKindKey` / `VmDoc` routing is removed). The whole `keylint.go` / `keylint_test.go` yaml.v3 `KnownFields` unknown-key linter is deleted ŌĆö CUE's closed-schema check is the real unknown-key gate now, so its self-decoding-types carve-out is gone too. Also deleted: the orphaned `group_spec.go`, `module_spec.go`, `resource_config.go`, `target_spec.go` hand structs the generated `spec` package supersedes.

**No authored wire key changed ŌĆö there is NO schema-version bump and NO `charly migrate` step.** This cutover replaces HOW the grammar is sourced (hand structs + hand vocab lists ŌåÆ generated-from-CUE), not the grammar itself: every `charly.yml` that loaded before loads identically after, and the "legacy forms hard-rejected" above are the pre-existing pre-`#NodeDoc` shapes already gated by the unified-node migration, not a new wire change. `LatestSchemaVersion()` stays **`2026.169.0004`** and the migration registry is untouched. Runtime class: `go test ./...` (the `gen_repro` reproducibility gate, the `reserved_registry` bijection gates, the CUE corpus + closedness tests), `task cue:gen` reproducing the committed `spec` package, and `charly box validate` across the superproject + every `box/<distro>` submodule. Bumps the `plugins` gitlink to the matching skill sweep.

### 2026-06-20 ŌĆö fix(chrome-cdp): forward caller flags via "$@" so Chrome's welcome dialog is suppressed and it starts maximized (`v2026.171.0416`)

The `chrome-wrapper` exec block lacked `"$@"`, so the launch flags the supervised `[program:chrome]` service (`selkies-core`) and `chrome-restart` passed were silently DROPPED ŌĆö on the selkies streaming desktops Chrome showed its first-run "welcome / make default" dialog and opened un-maximized. Fix: the launch flags now live in the wrapper itself (single source) and `"$@"` forwards any caller flags; `chrome-restart` and the `selkies-core` chrome service are simplified to call the bare wrapper. The old callers' `--force-renderer-accessibility` (inert under the dropped-flags bug, so production Chrome never actually had it) is intentionally NOT restored ŌĆö CDP automation does not need forced renderer a11y. Adds 3 deterministic `selkies-core` checks that FAIL without the fix: `selkies-core-chrome-launch-flags` (`--no-first-run` + `--start-maximized` in the live `/proc/<pid>/cmdline`), `selkies-core-chrome-maximized` (CDP-measured window Ōēł screen ŌåÆ `MAXOK`, proving maximize took effect not merely the flag), `selkies-core-frame-not-uniform` (real composited frame, not a black void ŌĆö closes the same false-green gap the `agent-check` leaves under `--no-agent`). Verified on the `check-selkies-labwc-pod` bed (180 steps, 0 failed; all 3 new checks PASS on a fresh rebuild) + a live screenshot of the maximized welcome-free Chrome. The selkies-KDE flavor has a separate no-systemd-user session instability that blocks ITS bed (HELD as a dedicated effort ŌĆö see the `selkies-kde-kwin-instability` memory: systemd1 `/bin/false` storm + wl-paste/wlr-data-control leak both fixed there, chrome CDP `unix_wait_for_peer` needs a real systemd-user); this fix is the shared chrome candy, proven on the labwc flavor. candy `chrome-cdp` ŌåÆ 2026.170.2101, `selkies-core` ŌåÆ 2026.170.2327.

### 2026-06-19 ŌĆö feat(charly)!: unified name-first node model for all of charly.yml + GPU auto-preemptible arbitration (`v2026.170.1105`)

charly.yml collapses to ONE name-first node model ŌĆö every entity, bundle member,
plan step, and data field is a `<name>: {<kind>: ŌĆ”, <child-nodes>}` node, one
`#Node` CUE schema at every depth (CLOSED, fully validated before anything
executes). `deploy:`ŌåÆ`bundle:`, `charly deploy`ŌåÆ`charly bundle`,
`DeploymentNode`ŌåÆ`BundleNode`. Venue + membership now come from TREE POSITION ŌĆö
the authored `on:`/`pod:`(step)/`peer:`/`nested:`/`target:` keys are REMOVED; a
step nested under a member runs on that member, a resource node placed under
another deploys into it. `${HOST:<member>}` (`:<port>` for a host-reachable
endpoint) is the SOLE cross-member address, superseding
`${PEER_HOST}`/`${PEER_ENDPOINT}`. A new `agent_provisioned: true` tree-child flag
marks agent-built bed pods (foldMembers skips them ŌĆö the iterate-benchmark
contract). An idempotent `charly migrate` step (+ registry HEAD bump) synthesizes
all of it from any legacy config. CUE stays the closed schema authority.

GPU resource-arbitration robustness: a pod that USES the nvidia GPU device
auto-claims `requires_shared:[nvidia-gpu]` (`acquireResourceForClaimant` ŌåÆ
`withImpliedGPUShared`), so EVERY GPU consumer is a tracked, preemptable shared
claimant with no per-deploy config ŌĆö the `requires_exclusive:` arbiter then
gracefully preempts them and flips nvidiaŌåÆvfio fully automatically. The switch's
EBUSY refusal now NAMES the external holder (`formatNvidiaHolders` /
`discoverNvidiaHolders`) instead of a cryptic message.

R10 (fresh rebuild, RTX 4080): `check-cross-pod-cdp` PASS; `check-selkies-kde-nvidia-vm`
from-box nested-pod deploy + nvidiaŌåÆvfio switch + in-guest GPU live-proven; a
`gpu-holder` ordinary pod auto-claimed + preempted on-card; full bed roster (24
beds + 3 cross beds) proven on the unified loader; `charly box validate` exit 0
across all 6 repos; `go test`/`golangci` green. Known immediate-next cutovers:
box-submodule candy `@github` pins ŌåÆ `charly box reconcile` to this tag; the
selkies-kde desktop stream (:3000) needs GSettings schemas + an
xdg-desktop-portal rootless-fuse fix (a selkies-kde candy issue, not this change).

### 2026-06-17 ŌĆö chore(hooks): end-of-turn reminder gains an autonomy anchor (`v2026.168.1602`)

`end-of-turn-challenge.sh` (the `Stop` hook) was rewritten to emphasize
autonomous completion: if ANY cutover / task / TODO is still unfinished the
answer to "should I continue?" is ALWAYS YES ŌĆö keep going automatically (Hard
Cutover runs end-to-end through R10; disposable:true targets need no extra
permission), never stopping merely to ask whether to proceed; EVERY failure /
warning / anomaly must get a proper RCA + real fix per CLAUDE.md (R1), with
"flake" / "transient" / "out of scope" / "follow-up" forbidden (R2); and the hook
STOPs only when all work is done AND verified, or when a genuine, unresolvable
question blocks (then ONE specific question). Still soft (exit 0) and
pointer-shaped ŌĆö no rule bodies restated. The `/charly-internals:agents` Hooks
doctrine row summarizes the hook's re-audit role and stays accurate (the autonomy
anchor is a behavioral anchor it does not enumerate). Hook-script change class.

### 2026-06-17 ŌĆö docs+chore(changelog,hooks): per-repo monthly `CHANGELOG/` + full-roster compliance reminder + deterministic CHANGELOG gate (`v2026.168.1551`)

History moved from a single ever-growing root `CHANGELOG.md` to a per-repo
`CHANGELOG/` directory with one file per calendar month (`YYYY-MM.md`). The
7937-line root monolith was split along its existing `## YYYY-MM` markers into
`CHANGELOG/{2026-06,2026-05,2026-04}.md` (all 221 dated monthly entries preserved
verbatim); its 3 trailing non-month thematic sections (engineering cautionary
tales, early schema cutovers, relocated layer/image/command history) were dropped
as outdated; the monolith was deleted (hard cutover). Every repository in the project ŌĆö superproject, `plugins`,
`pkg/{arch,fedora,debian}`, `box/{arch,cachyos,debian,fedora,ubuntu}` ŌĆö now keeps
its **own** `CHANGELOG/` (each seeded with a `README.md` index + this month's
file); history is repo-scoped, never centralized.

The two soft compliance hooks were strengthened to drive a SECOND-PASS
verification (operator: "a REMINDER not a full duplication"):
`runtime-verification-reminder.sh` now names the full R0ŌĆōR10 + RDD + ADE roster
as terse second-pass *triggers* (pointers to CLAUDE.md, never rule-body copies),
and `end-of-turn-challenge.sh` now prompts a re-audit of every code/config change
against R0ŌĆōR10 + the Acceptance checklist and a check that each changed repo
recorded its current-month `CHANGELOG/` entry. `pre-commit-gate.sh` gains a
deterministic gate: a runtime-tier commit (`fully tested and validated` /
`analysed on a live system`) in a repo that tracks `CHANGELOG/` must stage a
`CHANGELOG/YYYY-MM.md` entry ŌĆö pure submodule-pointer-bump commits and
documentation-tier commits are exempt; the `DOC_PATH` docs-classifier is
unchanged (a `CHANGELOG/YYYY-MM.md` path already matches its `.md` clause). The
"Hooks doctrine" was amended to bless the fuller pointer roster (the quantitative
"Ōēż10 lines / one behavioral anchor" caps are lifted) while keeping its
anti-duplication core ŌĆö hooks still never restate rule *bodies*; CLAUDE.md
remains the single source. Doc-only across `*.md` + the three hook scripts (the
hook-script change class); the new gate self-verified the superproject commit.

### 2026-06-17 ŌĆö fix(selkies-kde): KWin wl-probes source the live compositor env (`eval`, not `check`) (`v2026.168.1408`)

The selkies-kde streaming desktop's `charly check wl` probes
(`kde-wl-keyboard-wtype`, `kde-wl-toplevel-via-kdotool`) failed on the KWin
session: `wtype` reported "Compositor does not support the virtual keyboard
protocol" and `kdotool` reported "org.kde.KWin was not provided".

Root cause: `wlCompositorEnvPrelude` (wl.go) is designed to source the running
compositor's live `WAYLAND_DISPLAY` + `DBUS_SESSION_BUS_ADDRESS` from
`/proc/<pid>/environ` ŌĆö KWin (started via `startplasma-wayland` under
`dbus-run-session`) renders into `wayland-1` (pixelflux) and registers
`org.kde.KWin` on a RANDOM `/tmp/dbus-XXXXXX` bus, not the baked defaults. But the
prelude applied the sourced exports with `check "$(...)"` instead of
`eval "$(...)"`; `check` is not a command, so the exports silently dropped and the
probe fell back to `wayland-0` + the baked `/tmp/dbus-session`, where wtype's
virtual-keyboard protocol is absent and `org.kde.KWin` is unregistered. One
`check`->`eval` typo broke BOTH the keyboard and the window probes at once.

Fix: `check`->`eval` in `wlCompositorEnvPrelude`. RDD-proven on a live selkies-kde
pod (wtype "Typed 6 characters"; kdotool listed the live KWin windows). The
kde-selkies supervisorctl-status check is marked `context: runtime` to match its
sibling (supervisord runs only in a live deploy). R5 claim-keyed sweep: the same
`eval`->`check` corruption in the secrets / direnv / charly-config / layer
SKILL.md `.envrc` / `.secrets` / direnv-hook examples was fixed in the plugins
repo (documentation reviewed).

R10: `check-selkies-kde-pod` PASS (10 steps; the 5 `kde-wl-*` probes green)
through the fresh-rebuild gate, run three times. Regression guard in
`wl_kwin_test.go` asserts the prelude sources via `eval` and never `check`.

### 2026-06-17 ŌĆö fix(check): committed-APK checks anchor to the authoring candy ŌĆö fail hard, no fallback (`v2026.168.1403`)

The android-emulator-pod bed's `adb: install` / `appium: install-app` checks
(android-emulator-layer's `apk: ./tests/data/ApiDemos-debug.apk`) resolved the
fixture cwd-relative and died with `open ./tests/data/...: no such file` ŌĆö only
under a `box/<distro>` bed run, never in the unit tests (which passed the Origin
in by hand).

Two root causes, both masked by a silent cwd-relative fall-through in
`resolveCheckApk` (and by an override-fallback patch that, it turned out, never
even executed for this bug ŌĆö `resolveCheckApk` returned on the empty-origin guard
long before reaching it):

1. **The per-step `Op.Origin` was never stamped.** The authoring candy's origin
   lives ONCE on the baked `LabeledDescription` group, not per-step in the OCI
   label; `RunPlan`/`runUnit` dispatched each step's `Op` without re-stamping
   `op.Origin = fs.origin`, so `resolveCheckApk` saw an empty `c.Origin` and could
   not key `CandyDirs`.
2. **`charly check feature run` never populated `CandyDirs`.** Only `charly check
   live` built the candyŌåÆsource-dir map, so the same committed-APK check passed
   under check-live yet failed (`0 candies scanned`) under feature-run ŌĆö cascading
   into 36 downstream appium failures against a then-absent ApiDemos.

Fix ŌĆö fail hard, no obfuscating fallback:

- `description_run.go`: stamp `op.Origin = fs.origin` onto every dispatched `Op`.
- `check_cmd.go`: a shared `attachCheckRunnerContext` helper wires identity +
  `CandyDirs` for BOTH `charly check live` AND `charly check feature run`, so the
  two can never diverge again (R3 ŌĆö one anchoring path).
- `resolveApkPath` / `resolveCheckApk` / `candySourceDirs` now return errors and
  FAIL HARD on any unanchorable committed APK (non-candy origin, absent
  `CandyDirs` entry, candy-scan error, file missing under the candy tree) ŌĆö no
  silent cwd-relative pass-through, no `CHARLY_REPO_OVERRIDE` fallback.

R10: `check-android-emulator-pod` PASS (15/15 steps) through the fresh-rebuild
gate (feature-run 260 passed / 0 failed / 20 skipped); `check-selkies-kde-pod`
PASS (shared-runner regression check). Regression guard
`TestRunPlan_StampsStepOrigin` fails without the origin stamp.

### 2026-06-17 ŌĆö fix(candy): unsloth-studio installs the Studio CLI via the official installer (`v2026.168.1135`)

The supervised `unsloth studio` service FATAL'd "can't find command 'unsloth'":
the prior fix wrongly assumed the `unsloth` pip package ships the Studio CLI ŌĆö it

`~/.unsloth/studio` venv at build so the supervised launch is immediate) with a

installer builds its GGUF engine from source and on Arch does not auto-install
them); the service execs the launcher by absolute path. R10:

### 2026-06-17 ŌĆö fix(candy): java-openjdk resolves /usr/bin/java on Arch (`v2026.168.1031`)

On Arch/CachyOS `/usr/bin/java` symlinks through `/usr/lib/jvm/default-runtime`,
which ships UNSET (-> `/dev/null`) until `archlinux-java set` runs, so the absolute
launcher failed with ENOTDIR. Added a guarded `archlinux-java set` (a no-op on
Fedora/Debian/Ubuntu, which wire update-alternatives at install) pointing the
system default at JDK 21, and cleaned a malformed run-step whose prose leaked a
`command=...` body. analysed on a live system: `check-android-emulator-pod`
(cachyos) built fresh and ran check-image + check-live ŌĆö all java-openjdk checks
PASS; the bed's full gate did not complete due to the then-unfixed committed-APK
fixture-path bug (its own cutover, since landed as `v2026.168.1403`).

### 2026-06-17 ŌĆö fix(candy): redis-responds probe is host-independent (`v2026.168.0957`)

The `redis-responds` check ran `redis-cli` from the HOST against
`${HOST_PORT:6379}`; on a multi-service pod where the host port mapping is not
under test this is fragile. Probe redis INSIDE the container on its fixed port 6379
(`in_container: true`), proving the supervised `redis-server` answers regardless of
host remapping; the separate `redis-port-open` check still proves host TCP
reachability. R10: `check-cachyos-immich-ml-pod` PASS (10 steps, 128 check-live, 0
failed) through the fresh-rebuild gate.

### 2026-06-17 ŌĆö fix(candy): chrome/direnv/thunar check correctness (`v2026.168.0944`)

chrome: removed the `google-chrome-stable --version` check ŌĆö RDD on a live pod
proved that when chrome-cdp wraps the binary, `--version` LAUNCHES a full browser
and hangs ~125s, driving every desktop bed's check-live to the readiness cap; the
file/package/`.desktop` checks already prove chrome is installed. direnv: the
`/etc/profile.d/charly-direnv-<shell>.sh` drop-in said `check "$(direnv hook X)"` ŌĆö
`check` is no builtin, so direnv was never hooked and every login shell printed
"check: command not found"; fixed to `eval`, with discriminating checks. thunar:
`package_map {fedora: Thunar}` (the Fedora rpm capitalizes the name). R10:
`check-sway-browser-vnc-pod` PASS (10 steps; check-live 34s vs the prior 30-min
cap-kill) through the fresh-rebuild gate.

### 2026-06-17 ŌĆö fix(candy): cross-distro nested-container + gocryptfs/supervisord robustness (`v2026.168.0927`)

container-nesting on Debian/Ubuntu: add `libcap2-bin` (provides `setcap(8)`, which
Fedora/Arch ship transitively but Debian/Ubuntu do not ŌĆö without it the setcap RUN
step exits 127 and fails the build); `chmod u-s` newuidmap/newgidmap (Debian/Ubuntu
ship them setuid-root, which fails in a nested rootless userns when combined with
file capabilities ŌĆö match Fedora/Arch's cap-only posture); resolve the uid-1000
user via getent. gocryptfs: widen the version-banner regex (newer gocryptfs drops
the leading `v`). supervisord: accept `XDG_RUNTIME_DIR` = `/tmp/xdg-runtime` OR
`/tmp` and test by exit status. R10: PASS on `check-fedora-coder-pod` (278),
`check-charly-fedora-pod` (106), `check-debian-coder-pod` (272),
`check-ubuntu-coder-pod` (272) through the fresh-rebuild gate.

### 2026-06-17 ŌĆö fix(check): load-robust check-live ŌĆö per-probe never-hang + generous PollHeavy bound (`v2026.168.0829`)

Under heavy parallel load a slow-but-progressing `charly check live` pass was
SIGKILLed: `stepReady` ran the WHOLE multi-probe pass under a 120s `PerAttempt` and
the probes shared one ctx with no per-probe bound, so a 100+-probe pass needing
>120s was killed every tick to the 30-min cap (bed FAIL, empty step log). Fix: a
per-probe never-hang (each probe attempt under
`context.WithTimeout(ctx, probeNeverHang)`, honoring a longer author `timeout:`) so
a wedged probe is cancelled individually and the pass continues; and PollHeavy now
uses a new `PerAttemptHeavy` (15m default; config + env + closed `#Readiness`
schema) so the whole subprocess is never guillotined mid-pass. R10:
`check-fedora-coder-pod` (278 steps) under load avg ~30 PASS ŌĆö check-live 217s,
feature-run 215s, feature-run-rebuild 219s (all >120s); new tests fail when the fix
is neutralized.

### 2026-06-17 ŌĆö fix(gpu)!: device_lock-safe group-aware GPU driver switch + wedge poisoning + `charly vm gpu recover` (`v2026.168.0526`)

Root-caused and fixed the GPU driver-switch wedge that, in the prior campaign,
hung the host's nvidia card uninterruptibly and required a reboot.

**Root cause (source-confirmed against NVIDIA's open kernel modules
`kernel-open/nvidia/nv-pci.c`, then RDD-proven on the live RTX 4080 SUPER).** A
sysfs `unbind` of the `nvidia` driver fires `nv_pci_remove ŌåÆ
nv_pci_remove_helper(block_if_gpu_in_use=TRUE)`, which ŌĆö when `nvl->usage_count
!= 0` (any open `/dev/nvidia*` fd, live CUDA context, or
`nvidia_uvm`/`nvidia_modeset`/`nvidia_drm` still attached) ŌĆö blocks forever in
`while (usage_count != 0) os_delay(500)`. The Linux PCI core holds the
per-device `device_lock` (`dev->mutex`, uninterruptible) across the entire
`.remove`, so every later bind/reset/remove on the device serializes behind it
in unkillable `D` state. Recovery is reboot-only: no userspace primitive
releases a held `device_lock`. It is **not** power/runtime-PM related (a
disproven earlier hypothesis); `nv_pci_shutdown` passes `block=FALSE` so host
reboot/shutdown never wedges.

**The fix (prevention + cascade containment, not avoidance):**
- `charly/gpu_driver_switch.go` rewritten ŌĆö the switch is now **group-aware**
  (flips EVERY function of the IOMMU group: displayŌåÆnvidia/vfio,
  HDMI-audioŌåÆsnd_hda_intel/vfio; a VFIO group is guest-usable only when all
  members are vfio-bound) and the nvidiaŌåÆvfio detach uses **`modprobe -r`**
  (module-refcount-guarded ŌåÆ `EBUSY` fast-fail if a client holds the GPU; it can
  never reach the blocking `.remove` loop) ŌĆö it NEVER sysfs-unbinds a busy
  nvidia. `runGPUSwitchScript` is bounded (context deadline + `WaitDelay`) so a
  GSP-teardown stall frees charly + the arbiter lock instead of blocking forever;
  a confirmed wedge returns the new `errGPUSwitchWedged` sentinel.
- `charly/preempt.go` ŌĆö on a wedge the arbiter **POISONS** the GPU resource
  (a boot-id-keyed marker under the preemption dir) and refuses it to every later
  claimant, including `reconcileStranded`, so a wedged card can never be handed
  out to produce a second `D`-state; the poison clears on reboot.
- `charly/vm_gpu_cmd.go` ŌĆö `charly vm gpu status` now reports **per-function**
  driver + IOMMU group + mode and flags a wedged/poisoned card; new `charly vm
  gpu recover` rebinds an unbound/half-switched card to vfio-pci but, on a true
  wedge, reports reboot-required and attempts nothing (a bind would re-wedge).
  `charly vm gpu mode` switches the whole group.

**Removed (R5 claim-keyed sweep).** The load-bearing comment in
`gpu_driver_switch.go` asserting "Only the DISPLAY function is ever flipped; the
sibling AUDIO function stays on vfio-pci ŌĆ” RDD-proven" is DELETED ŌĆö it was false
(the real constraint is IOMMU-group VFIO viability, and the wedge was never
about module liveness). The vfio/GPU model in `/charly-vm:vm` (new "GPU
driver-mode switch" section, the owner), `/charly-internals:disposable`, and
`/charly-check:check` is rewritten to the source-confirmed model. Memory:
`gpu-driver-switch-wedge-rca.md`.

### 2026-06-16 ŌĆö fix(preempt): correct concurrent shared-GPU arbitration ŌĆö serialized flip + process-liveness lease reconciliation (`v2026.167.1853`)

Two coupled fixes so multiple `requires_shared: [nvidia-gpu]` beds (e.g. comfyui +
jupyter-ml) BUILD and RUN concurrently while only the brief GPU driver flip is
gated ŌĆö never the pods themselves.

**1. Serialize the flip (the `driver=unbound` race).** A 16-way fan-out surfaced
`check-cachyos-comfyui-pod` failing instantly at acquisition:
`switch-to-nvidia FAILED: 0000:01:00.0 driver=unbound`. `ResourceArbiter`'s three
mutating methods (`AcquireShared` / `AcquireExclusive` / `ReleaseClaimant`) ran the
whole load-ledger ŌåÆ decide ŌåÆ GPU-driver-flip ŌåÆ save-ledger sequence with NO lock,
so two claimants starting together both began the flip ŌĆö one unbound vfio-pci while
the other was mid-bind ŌåÆ the device was left `driver=unbound`, the nvidia bind
failed, and both raced the lease-ledger write. Fix: the three methods now take a
blocking lock (the unified `acquireFileLock` primitive ŌĆö filelock.go) on
`~/.local/share/charly/preemption/.lock` around the whole acquire/release. The
first claimant flips the card and records its lease; the second blocks, then finds
the card already nvidia (idempotent ŌĆö no re-flip) and just refcounts. No
re-entrancy / self-deadlock: holder stop/start is in-process, nested `charly`
subprocesses are env-guarded (`CHARLY_PREEMPT_LEASE`) before any arbiter method, and
`reconcileStranded`/`removeLease` use `loadLedger`/`saveLedger` directly. Fifth site
on the one flock primitive (per-bed, deploy-config, build, harness/ledger, arbiter).

**2. Process-liveness lease reconciliation (the concurrent-shared CLOBBER the lock
EXPOSED).** Serializing the flip let a live concurrent R10 run far enough to surface
a pre-existing bug from the GPU-switch cutover: `reconcileStranded` (run at the top
of every acquire) judged a lease "stranded" via `a.running(lz.Claim)` ŌĆö "is the
claimant POD running?". But a TRANSIENT bed lease is created at the FIRST step of
the run, minutes BEFORE its pod is built/deployed; so the second concurrent
claimant's `reconcileStranded` saw the first, still-building bed's lease (pod not up)
and garbage-collected it as "claimant gone" ŌĆö two shared claimants clobbered each
other's leases (`leases=1`, never the refcount of 2). Fix: a lease's liveness is its
OWNER, not its pod. New `leaseLive` helper keys a TRANSIENT lease on its owning
process (the long-lived `charly check run` orchestrator) via PID + `/proc`
start-time (a PID-reuse guard so a crashed owner whose PID was recycled still reads
as gone ŌĆö crash-recovery must not hinge on luck), and a PERSISTENT lease on
`a.running(Claim) || ownerAlive` (the OR covers a `charly start` creator's own
bring-up window). `leaseLive` is used by BOTH `reconcileStranded` AND
`Status` (`charly preempt status`), so the display never disagrees with the GC
(R3/R5 ŌĆö one predicate, both surfaces). The lease records `OwnerPID`/`OwnerStart` at
creation (outermost process only ŌĆö nested subprocesses skip the arbiter). And
`reconcileStranded` now routes its teardown through the shared `releaseLeaseEffects`
(extracted from `ReleaseClaimant`, R3) so a genuinely crashed shared-GPU bed also
flips the card back instead of leaving it nvidia.

Follow-up (own cutover, R2 ŌĆö not this change): `AcquireExclusive` unconditionally
drops overlapping shared leases (exclusive-wins), which would yank a still-building
shared bed's lease ŌĆö by-design exclusive-wins semantics, tracked separately.

Regression coverage: `TestArbiter_TransientLeaseLiveOwnerNotReconciled` (a live-owner
transient lease whose pod is not running is NOT reconciled ŌĆö fails under the old
pod-running predicate), `TestArbiter_TransientLeaseDeadOwnerReconciled` (PID-reuse
guard via start-time mismatch), `TestArbiter_TwoConcurrentSharedLeasesCoexist`
(refcount=2, token nvidia).

R10 (`fully tested and validated`): `go test ./...` + `go vet` PASS (incl. 3 new
arbiter regressions); `task build:charly` fresh (`2026.167.1703`). Concurrent live
R10 of `check-cachyos-comfyui-pod` + `check-cachyos-jupyter-ml-pod` (both
`requires_shared: [nvidia-gpu]`, launched together from one `box/cachyos` project
dir): BOTH rc=0, all 10 steps `ok: true` incl. the `update` fresh-rebuild gate;
~6 min wall for BOTH (overlapped ŌĆö comfyui 168s, jupyter-ml 356s, wall Ōēł max not
sum, so the pods ran concurrently); a SINGLE gated `vfioŌåÆnvidia` flip with the
nvidia-gpu refcount peaking at TWO coexisting active shared leases (the clobber is
gone); `driver=unbound` observations during the run: 0; post-run the card
auto-flipped back to `vfio-pci` with no leases left.

### 2026-06-16 ŌĆö feat(build): version-keyed candy staging `.build/_candy/<candy>.<version>/` + `charly clean` retention (`v2026.167.1703`)

Replaces the single shared `.build/_layers/<candy>/` staging dir with a
VERSION-keyed `.build/_candy/<candy>.<version>/` (the candy's CalVer). Different
candy versions now occupy DISTINCT dirs, which fixes a crossover the atomic-swap
(`v2026.167.1601`) alone did not: two concurrent builds in one project dir that
resolve the SAME candy at DIFFERENT versions (e.g. divergent `@github` pins across
boxes) previously shared `_layers/<candy>/` and got last-writer-wins ŌĆö one build
silently COPYed the wrong version. Each version keyed to its own dir makes both
correct.

Cache-neutral by construction: a candy's CalVer changes iff the candy changes, so
the Containerfile COPY path (`.build/_candy/<name>.<version>/`) moves exactly when
its content does ŌĆö podman's content+instruction cache still hits on unchanged
candies. Containerfile generation verified byte-identical across repeat generates.

The BOX build dir stays un-versioned (`.build/{box}/`): a box's
`EffectiveVersion` is its highest candy version, so versioning the box dir would
change every box-level COPY path on ANY candy bump ŌåÆ full box rebuild
(cache-hostile, against the build-speed goal). The box dir's own artifacts are
atomic single-version writes (no glob, no crossover), so versioning it buys
nothing correctness-wise. Crossover prevention lives where the bug class was: the
candy-derived, glob-installed staging.

`charly clean` now prunes outdated `.build/_candy/<candy>.<oldversion>/` dirs
(newest `keep_images` per candy ŌĆö the build-staging counterpart to image-tag
retention) AND removes the superseded `.build/_layers/` dir (unconditional, like
the makepkg sweep). The same prune auto-runs after `charly box build`
(`pruneBuildCandyDirs`).

R10 (`fully tested and validated`): `go test ./...` PASS incl. new
`TestPruneBuildCandyDirs` (keep-newest-N per candy + legacy `_layers` removal +
transient-temp skip) and the updated `TestCandyCopySource` (versioned path);
`task build:charly` fresh; generation verified deterministic; `charly clean`
live-verified (legacy `_layers` removed, current `_candy` kept); `check-pod` built
end-to-end from the versioned `_candy` dirs and PASSED (`ok:true`, `steps=10`,
0 `_candy` COPY errors, 79s).

### 2026-06-16 ŌĆö fix(build): dev-localpkg staging clears stale CalVer ŌĆö regression from the atomic-`.build/` cutover (`v2026.167.1638`)

The atomic-`.build/` cutover (`v2026.167.1601`) dropped the per-image
`os.RemoveAll(imageDir)` at the top of `generateContainerfile` (it raced
concurrent shared-base builds), reasoning that stale leftovers are harmless
because the Containerfile COPYs by name. That holds for fragments/routes/inline ŌĆö
but NOT for the **dev-local-pkg charly toolchain**: `renderLocalPkgImageDevInstall`
stages the locally-built package into `.build/<image>/_localpkg/<candy>/` and the
Containerfile installs via a GLOB (`dnf install /tmp/charly-pkgs/*.rpm` /
`pacman -U ŌĆ”/*.pkg.tar.zst`). Without the wipe, successive `task build:charly`
runs accumulated multiple CalVer builds of the package in that dir, so the glob
matched two versions ŌåÆ `cannot install both opencharly-ŌĆ”1518 and ŌĆ”1343:
conflicting requests` (fedora) / `duplicate target` (arch) on every charly-
toolchain image (`charly-fedora`, `githubrunner`, `charly-selftest`, `charly-arch`).
The 5-fedora R10 of `v2026.167.1601` missed it because those beds don't install
the charly PACKAGE via the glob; the 16-way fan-out surfaced it.

Fix: `renderLocalPkgImageDevInstall` now stages into a per-process temp dir and
installs it via `installDirAtomic` (the same `renameat2(RENAME_EXCHANGE)` swap as
`_layers`) ŌĆö the stage dir is REPLACED each generate, so only the CURRENT CalVer
is ever present, and the swap stays race-free under concurrent builds.

R10 (`fully tested and validated`): `go test ./...` + `go vet` PASS;
`task build:charly` fresh (`2026.167.1602`); `check-charly-fedora-pod` (the exact
bed that hit "conflicting requests") re-run all green ŌĆö `ok: true`, `PASS
(steps=10)`, the conflict gone, and exactly one package staged
(`opencharly-2026.167.1602-1.fc43.x86_64.rpm`); run concurrently with the 16-way
fan-out's tail (live parallel-safety demonstration).

### 2026-06-16 ŌĆö fix(check): safe parallel `charly check` runs ŌĆö unified flock + race-free atomic `.build/` + DAG-aware build coordination (`v2026.167.1601`)

A hyper-parallel fan-out of all pod check beds (16 concurrent `charly check run`)
failed, and the RCA found TWO real shared-state races (NOT a "concurrency limit"):

1. **The `.build/_layers` race.** `.build/_layers` is a staging dir SHARED by
   every image in a project dir (not per-image). Concurrent `charly box build`
   processes in the same dir race: one's `cleanStaleBuildDirs` / `_layers`
   repopulation removes the dir mid-COPY of the other's `podman build` ŌĆö observed
   as `removing stale dir .build/_layers: directory not empty` and
   `COPY .build/_layers/rpmfusion/ /: no such file or directory` (`exit status
   125`). This is the same-project-dir `.build/` race the memory note flagged as
   "cross-image scope unverified" ŌĆö now confirmed: DISTINCT images in the same
   dir DO race on the shared `_layers`.
2. **The deploy-config lost-update race.** `saveDeployState` / `cleanDeployEntry`
   did an unprotected read-modify-write on the per-host deploy overlay
   (`~/.config/charly/charly.yml`); `charly config` / `charly start` took no lock
   at all (unlike `charly deploy add`, which already held the ledger lock). Two
   parallel beds could loadŌåÆmodifyŌåÆsave and silently drop each other's entry ŌĆö
   the truncation class the `loadDeployConfigForWrite` docstring warns about.

A separate trigger surfaced first and masked these: a YAML syntax error
introduced into `candy/container-nesting/charly.yml` (an unquoted `command:`
scalar containing `cut -d: -f1` ŌĆö the colon-space is the YAML "mapping values
not allowed" trigger) aborted every bed's candy scan in ~1s. Fixed by
single-quoting; that fix lands with the container-nesting cluster-B cutover.

**Fix, part 1 ŌĆö ONE unified flock primitive** (`charly/filelock.go`,
`acquireFileLock(path, blocking)`), replacing the two pre-existing ad-hoc flock
copies and serving every serialization site. `syscall.Flock` now lives in
exactly one file. The four call sites:

| Site | Lock file | Mode | Prevents |
|---|---|---|---|
| per-bed | `.check/<bed>/.lock` | fail-fast (`LOCK_NB`) | a 2nd `charly check run` of the SAME bed clobbering the 1st (its pre-run `charly remove --purge` / `charly vm destroy` would wipe the live target mid-test) |
| per-image build | `<dir>/.build/.locks/<image>.lock` | blocking | concurrent COLD rebuilds of the SAME image ŌĆö see part 3 |
| deploy-config | `~/.config/charly/charly.yml.lock` | blocking | the lost-update on the shared deploy overlay |
| harness | `.check/<score>/.lock` | fail-fast | (migrated ŌĆö `acquireHarnessLock` now delegates) |
| ledger | `~/.config/opencharly/installed/.lock` | blocking | (migrated ŌĆö `AcquireLedgerLock` now delegates) |

**Fix, part 2 ŌĆö race-free, deterministic `.build/` generation**
(`charly/build_stage_atomic.go` + `generate.go`). The shared `.build/` staging is
made concurrency-safe by ATOMIC writes, NOT by serializing the build (serializing
cold builds ŌĆö the long pole ŌĆö would be catastrophic for wall-clock). Every shared
write is atomic + idempotent + byte-deterministic, so a concurrent `podman build`
always reads a COMPLETE artifact and podman's content+instruction-keyed cache
still hits: the destructive `os.RemoveAll(_layers)`/`RemoveAll(imageDir)` are
gone; `_layers` is rebuilt in a temp dir and installed via
`renameat2(RENAME_EXCHANGE)`; the Containerfile, init fragments, traefik routes,
context-ignore, and content-addressed inline staging are written temp-then-rename;
`cleanStaleBuildDirs` skips the `_`/`.`-prefixed staging dirs (`_layers`,
`_buildconfig`, `.locks`). Containerfiles are confirmed byte-identical across
repeat generations (the cache-miss-avoidance the determinism guarantees).

**Fix, part 3 ŌĆö DAG-aware build coordination: serialize the shared intermediates,
parallelize the fan-out.** A PER-IMAGE build lock (keyed by image name under
`.build/.locks/`) is held across each image's build. When many beds in one project
dir start at once, the FIRST to reach a shared intermediate (a base like `fedora`,
or an auto-intermediate) cold-builds it ONCE while the others block on THAT image's
lock and then cache-HIT it ŌĆö so a shared base is built once, never N├Ś redundant
cold builds ŌĆö while each distinct LEAF image takes its own lock so the leaves'
(cold) builds run FULLY PARALLEL. There is deliberately no per-dir build lock:
serializing the whole build phase would stall the parallel cold leaf builds.
Distinct project dirs (worktrees / box submodules) have distinct `.build/` trees ŌåÆ
distinct locks ŌåÆ unaffected.

R10 (`fully tested and validated`): `go test ./...` PASS (incl. new
`TestAtomicWriteFile_*` / `TestInstallDirAtomic_*` / `TestAcquireFileLock_*`);
`task build:charly` (binary fresh); Containerfile generation verified
deterministic (byte-identical across repeat generates). Per-bed lock ŌĆö two
